<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крушить.html>круши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krušénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>accident, crash; collapse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езда</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krušénije</b> pójezda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">train crash</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krušénije</b> nadéžd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ruin of one's hopes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпе́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крушение.html>круше́ние</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poterpétʹ <b>krušénije</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be wrecked; to have an accident (train, ship, plane, etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*krušiti</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to destroy, to shatter</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kryló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылатый.html>крыла́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krylátyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>winged
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылатый.html>крыла́тая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krylátaja rakéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cruise missile</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылатый.html>крыла́тые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krylátyje slová</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> expressions, pithy saying, catch-words, winged words</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***крыло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло</a> (1499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kridlo</i>. <i>Ы</i> probably appeared by the influence of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kryló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́лья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыла́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́льев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыл</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Poetic.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>

<li>fender, mudguard <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cover over a bicycle or motorcycle wheel</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> faction</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крылышко.html>кры́лышко</a> (10042)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kryló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ышко</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yško</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылышко.html>кры́лышко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krýlyško</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылышко.html>кры́лышка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылышко.html>кры́лышки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крылышко.html>кры́лышек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>крыло́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kryló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: (small) wing</li></ol>

***крыса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́са</a> (4165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́са</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krýsa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́сы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́с</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водяной.html>водяна́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́са</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vodjanája krýsa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">water rat; water vole</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an unimportant or unpleasant person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:канцелярский.html>канцеля́рская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́са</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kanceljárskaja krýsa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">office drudge; pen pusher</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a thief who steals from his fellows or informs against them; a rat</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">video games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> camper</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***крыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a> (17752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kryti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыть.html>покры́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover, to roof (a house); to thatch, to tile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шифер.html>ши́фером</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>krytʹ</b> šíferom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to slate</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to coat <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with paint</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to cover, to trump <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in card games</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нечего.html>не́чем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú néčem <b>krytʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he hasn't a leg to stand on, there's nothing he can say to that</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">he has no (good) card to cover</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scold, to rail <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to swear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mount (an animal to mate)</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>кры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыться.html>кры́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krýtʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:покрыться.html>покры́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie, to be, to be concealed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыться.html>кро́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:угроза.html>угро́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v jevó slováx <b>krójetsja</b> ugróza</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a hidden threat in his words</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> что́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыться.html>кро́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ štó-to <b>krójetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is something behind that</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>кры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ша</a> (895)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kryša</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kryti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cover, hide</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ša</i> (lt; <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-sja</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krýša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>крыш</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>roof
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:подвести.html>подвести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́шу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvodítʹ/podvestí dom pod <b>krýšu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>roof</b> the house</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> house, dwelling place</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> head, mind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>па́рня</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ша</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́дке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u párnja <b>krýša</b> ne v porjádke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the guy's not right in the <b>head</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> criminal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> protection; someone who provides protection</li></ol>

<p><b>кры́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ша.html>ша</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 4a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></b> ➔ кры + <b>ш</b> + <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> (суффиксальный).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-кры-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ш</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krjučók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючко́в</a></b>)

<p><b>крю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чо́к</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*b  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> знач. <i>крючкотвор</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склоняться.html>склоня́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образец.html>образцу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>существи́тельных</a> (<span title="в винительном падеже"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>?</span> — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючка́</a></i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючко́в</a></i>). 
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-крюч-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ок</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***кряду.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кряду.html>кряду</a> (26796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кряду.html>кря́ду</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krjádu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in succession, running
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восемь.html>во́семь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кряду.html>кря́ду</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vósemʹ časóv <b>krjádu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">eight hours running; eight hours straight</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>Две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночи</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кряду.html>кря́ду</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dve noči <b>krjádu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">two nights in a row</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:крякнуть.html>кря́кнуть</a> (8956)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">кря</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nu-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крякнуть.html>кря́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">krjáknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крякать.html>кря́кать</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кряхтеть.html>кряхте́ть</a> (7542)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крякать.html>кря́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krjákatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to quack, to grunt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>Polish Catholic priest</li></ol>

***ксерокс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́рокс</a> (24351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the brand name <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́рокс</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Kséroks</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Xerox</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́рокс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kséroks</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́рокса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́роксы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ксерокс.html>ксе́роксов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> photocopier, xerox <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">machine which reproduces documents by photographing the original over a glass plate and printing duplicates</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> photocopy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">copy made using a photocopier</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">копирова́льный <a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kopiroválʹnyj apparát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***кстати.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кстати.html>кста́ти</a> (610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">státi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dative singular of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">statʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кстати.html>кста́ти</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kstáti</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>to the point</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hedge</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> by the way, incidentally</li>
<li>as a matter of fact</li>
<li>opportunely, in the nick of time</li>
<li>apropos</li>
<li>besides, too, as well</li></ol>

<p><b>кста́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a> (46)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъto</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷis</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>who
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лал</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne znáju, <b>kto</b> éto sdélal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t know <b>who</b> did this.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kto</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(relative pronoun)</i> who
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>Тот</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лал</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tot, <b>kto</b> éto sdélal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The one <b>who</b> did it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(interrogative pronoun)</i> who
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kto</b> éto?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Who</b>’s this?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:косвенный.html>ко́свенных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падежа́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ния</a> <b>-ого</b>, <b>-ому</b>, <b>-ем</b>, <b>-ом</b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>Други́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специалист.html>специали́сты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выделять.html>выделя́ют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a> <b>-о</b><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | ru 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <b>-то</b><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | ru 2 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> им. <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падеже́</a>.
</p>

***куб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a> (7405)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed in the early 18th century from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kubus</i> or directly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cubus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύβος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúbos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">die, cube</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кубический.html>куби́ческий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cube <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">shape with six square sides</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cube <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">number raised to the third power</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бе</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dva v <b>kúbe</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">2<sup>3</sup></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кубату́ра</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kubatúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кубик.html>ку́бик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúbik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">кубъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kubŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drinking vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="defdate">[14th century]</span>, further origin uncertain.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kub</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooden dish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kubek</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bowl, cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">kub</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bowl, cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">kubk</i>.
</p><p>Per Vasmer, likely related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">कुम्भ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kumbha</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Avestan" class="extiw" title="w:Avestan">Avestan</a></span> <i class="Avst mention" lang="ae">𐬑𐬎𐬨𐬠𐬀‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ae-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xumba‎</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύμβος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúmbos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύβη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúbē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, also <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κύμβη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúmbē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>However Trubachev notes that there are no signs of a nasal vowel and reconstructs <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kubъ</i>, thus rejecting possible link to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kumbʰo-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kumbʰéh₂-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and proposing connection to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*koubʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>кубы́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>кубо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ку́бовый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boiler, still, large tank
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">перего́нный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">peregónnyj <b>kub</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">distillation <b>boiler</b></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кубово́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kubovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кубок.html>ку́бок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúbok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кубышка.html>кубы́шка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kubýška</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">potbellied vessel with a neck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ку́бовина</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kúbovina</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">convexity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ку́бовый <a href = vnd.unilang:краситель.html>краси́тель</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúbovyj krasítelʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vat dye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ку́бовый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúbovyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">related to dye vatting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kub</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">large tank, vat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see above.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>куб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куб.html>ку́бов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ку́бовый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vat dye, specifically alkaline solution of indigo prepared for dyeing</li>
<li>indigo <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
